  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({

  <span id="freeText10751011166630892368" style="display:none">Related games Fortnite, League of Legends, Dota 2, FIFA, Overwatch, CS:GO, Clash Royale, Hearthstone and F1 series<br /><br />“How can I become a professional esports player?”<br />“How can I make a living playing esports?”<br />“What is the lifespan of an esports game?”<br />“What are the most popular esports?”<br /><br />These are just some of the questions I have been asked over the last five years. With the boom of the esports industry, everyone wants to know how they can be part of it. In this book, I have answered those questions, and dozens more, based on my years of experience working in the professional esports scene as a team manager. <br /><br />In this book, you will find no topic was off limits. I talk about the past, present, and future of esports and different aspects of the professional gaming industry at large.</span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2637792846" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1601688507644833937">О ЧЕМ КНИГА: <br/>Наконец то вышла первая нормальная книга про одну из самых быстрорастущих и многообещающих индустрий. Автор - менеджер одной из международных киберспортивных организаций и поэтому знает всю экосистему бизнеса изнутри. В книге вообще нет воды. Простыми словами объясняется, как устроен рынок, сколько зарабатывают спортсмены и команды, как организованы турниры. Ну и конечно автор делает свои предсказания о том, какое прекрасное будущее ждет киберспорт.<br/><br/>ГЛАВНЫЕ ВЫВОДЫ: <br/>- Индустрия набира</span>
  <span id="freeText1601688507644833937" style="display:none">О ЧЕМ КНИГА: <br />Наконец то вышла первая нормальная книга про одну из самых быстрорастущих и многообещающих индустрий. Автор - менеджер одной из международных киберспортивных организаций и поэтому знает всю экосистему бизнеса изнутри. В книге вообще нет воды. Простыми словами объясняется, как устроен рынок, сколько зарабатывают спортсмены и команды, как организованы турниры. Ну и конечно автор делает свои предсказания о том, какое прекрасное будущее ждет киберспорт.<br /><br />ГЛАВНЫЕ ВЫВОДЫ: <br />- Индустрия набирает обороты. Туда уже начинают приходить большие спонсоры и профессиональные инвесторы.<br /><br />- В киберспорте действуют те же самые правила, что и в других видах спорта. Одно дело часами играть дома в игрушки, а другое быть профессиональным киберспортсменом.<br /><br />- Пока мы еще не видим больших денег в киберспорте. Рост финансовых вливаний в индустрию отличается в разы по в сравнению с классическими видами спорта, такими как футбол или баскетбол. Одна из причин в том, что большинство руководителей компаний, которые распоряжаются крупными бюджетами – это люди старшего поколения, которые скорее всего не играли много в компьютерные игры в молодости. Скоро им на смену придет новое поколение, которое уже не представляет свою жизнь без компьютерных игр.</span>
  <a data-text-id="1601688507644833937" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_3150009747" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3150009747" />
    <a title="Bryant Wu" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/108004208-bryant-wu"><img alt="Bryant Wu" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/u_50x66-632230dc9882b4352d753eedf9396530.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3150009747?book_show_action=true">Jan 19, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Bryant Wu" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Bryant Wu" href="/user/show/108004208-bryant-wu">Bryant Wu</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3150009747" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15597822333352220764">The best way to describe this book is that it is full of information but no insight. <br/><br/>The book has 4 main chapters but within each chapter are a seemingly random string of questions and answers that someone might type and read through a simple Google search. <br/><br/>Here is an example of how the book has information but no insight:<br/><br/>"there aren’t too many competitors in the Live Game Streaming industry. This may be because you need a lot of servers around the world to become a global player."<br/><br/>Information: n</span>
  <span id="freeText15597822333352220764" style="display:none">The best way to describe this book is that it is full of information but no insight. <br /><br />The book has 4 main chapters but within each chapter are a seemingly random string of questions and answers that someone might type and read through a simple Google search. <br /><br />Here is an example of how the book has information but no insight:<br /><br />"there aren’t too many competitors in the Live Game Streaming industry. This may be because you need a lot of servers around the world to become a global player."<br /><br />Information: not that many competitors<br />Insight: high server costs<br /><br />Surely there are more reasons for low number of competitors than just high server costs (e.g., network effects) As you can see, the book falls to give a strong POV on WHY things are the way they are.<br /><br />In summary, this book can serve as a useful starting point if you don't want to search Google yourself, but if you want something more, look elsewhere<br /></span>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('HQBCcyhtQXYuOyxephrn+u2V+LlWKhY4gcXRzghLidr+7UnZEVYGVV2XRvXIQmN3+yR6NU2aqhXs+oWlZIILHQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('9tE3GpKvdFrbvUn3lBQ4UCsD1KzswxBm0EkRC85+sy8VPDywq5QzeagRI1z6TLzdPbJWIPdzrEu9dkVgorcx6A==')})
  }

But it points to the direction of your goal.Entrepreneurs are lifelong learners and researchers.As an entrepreneur, As a producer, you give yourself to learning about the business system, your chosen industry, and your work environment.Don\'t buy into self-doubt. Self-doubt robs you of the inner energy to make concrete decisions. It destroys your dreams more than the actual risks involved in your business.The Entrepreneur mindset is decisive, open to learning and mistakes, accepts challenges, and takes responsibility. It is centered on improving one\'s skills.You can develop the mindset of an entrepreneur. Morale had deteriorated, competition was more intense, and technology was changing faster than at any time in the company\'s history. &quot;I knew there was nothing to be gained from arguing over the past,&quot; Iger writes. &quot;The only thing that mattered was the future, and I believed I had a clear idea of the direction Disney needed to go.&quot; It came down to three clear ideas: 1) Create the highest quality content Disney could produce. 2) Embrace and adopt technology instead of fighting it. Its value is nearly five times what it was when Iger took over, and Iger is recognized as one of the most innovative and successful CEOs of our time.\n\nNow, he\'s sharing the lessons he\'s learned while running Disney and leading its 200,000 employees--taking big risks in the face of historic disruption; learning to inspire the people who work for you; leading with fairness and communicating principles clearly. This book is about the relentless curiosity that has driven Iger for forty-five years, since the day he started as a studio supervisor at ABC. It\'s also about thoughtfulness and respect, and a decency-over-dollars approach that has become the bedrock of every project and partnership Iger pursues, from a deep friendship with Steve Jobs in his final years to an abiding love of the evolving Star Wars myth.\n\n&quot;Over the past fourteen years, I think I\'ve learned so much about what real leadership is,&quot; Iger writes. &quot;But I couldn\'t have articulated all of this until I lived it. <div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer17650963882613052976">Zoltán Andrejkovics born in 1985, Head of esports at Docler group, married and father of one. He always had an interest in fields of interpersonal psychology, team dynamics, competitive gaming and eSports. His professional experiences gave a lot of real life examples how team members could achieve real goals.</span>
